        }

          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





UAF bug in blink, it affects chromium from version 85 to 89.



<span class="line"><!---->UAF bug in blink, it affects chromium from version 85 to 89.<!----></span>



<br>





The problem is:



<span class="line"><!---->The problem is:<!----></span>



<br>





On CanvasRenderingContext2D constuctor, which hold a raw pointer ukm_recorder_ which will be freed on the Document destruct.



<span class="line"><!---->On CanvasRenderingContext2D constuctor, which hold a raw pointer ukm_recorder_ which will be freed on the Document destruct.<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/89.0.4389.88:third_party/blink/renderer/modules/canvas/canvas2d/canvas_rendering_context_2d.cc;l=155



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/89.0.4389.88:third_party/blink/renderer/modules/canvas/canvas2d/canvas_rendering_context_2d.cc;l=155"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/89.0.4389.88:third_party/blink/renderer/modules/canvas/canvas2d/canvas_rendering_context_2d.cc;l=155<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/89.0.4389.88:third_party/blink/renderer/core/dom/document.h;l=2081;



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/89.0.4389.88:third_party/blink/renderer/core/dom/document.h;l=2081;"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/89.0.4389.88:third_party/blink/renderer/core/dom/document.h;l=2081;<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





    #0 0x555fc9a02dbd in operator delete(void*) /b/s/w/ir/cache/builder/src/third_party/llvm/compiler-rt/lib/asan/asan_new_delete.cpp:160:3



<span class="line"><!---->    #0 0x555fc9a02dbd in operator delete(void*) /b/s/w/ir/cache/builder/src/third_party/llvm/compiler-rt/lib/asan/asan_new_delete.cpp:160:3<!----></span>



<br>





    #1 0x555fe0ea44ae in std::__1::default_delete<ukm::UkmRecorder>::operator()(ukm::UkmRecorder*) const buildtools/third_party/libc++/trunk/include/memory:2378:5



<span class="line"><!---->    #1 0x555fe0ea44ae in std::__1::default_delete&lt;ukm::UkmRecorder&gt;::operator()(ukm::UkmRecorder*) const buildtools/third_party/libc++/trunk/include/memory:2378:5<!----></span>



<br>





    #2 0x555fe0ea44ae in std::__1::unique_ptr<ukm::UkmRecorder, std::__1::default_delete<ukm::UkmRecorder> >::reset(ukm::UkmRecorder*) buildtools/third_party/libc++/trunk/include/memory:2633:7



<span class="line"><!---->    #2 0x555fe0ea44ae in std::__1::unique_ptr&lt;ukm::UkmRecorder, std::__1::default_delete&lt;ukm::UkmRecorder&gt; &gt;::reset(ukm::UkmRecorder*) buildtools/third_party/libc++/trunk/include/memory:2633:7<!----></span>



<br>





    #3 0x555fe0ea44ae in std::__1::unique_ptr<ukm::UkmRecorder, std::__1::default_delete<ukm::UkmRecorder> >::~unique_ptr() buildtools/third_party/libc++/trunk/include/memory:2587:19



<span class="line"><!---->    #3 0x555fe0ea44ae in std::__1::unique_ptr&lt;ukm::UkmRecorder, std::__1::default_delete&lt;ukm::UkmRecorder&gt; &gt;::~unique_ptr() buildtools/third_party/libc++/trunk/include/memory:2587:19<!----></span>



<br>





    #4 0x555fe0ea44ae in blink::Document::~Document() third_party/blink/renderer/core/dom/document.cc:908:1



<span class="line"><!---->    #4 0x555fe0ea44ae in blink::Document::~Document() third_party/blink/renderer/core/dom/document.cc:908:1<!----></span>



<br>





    #5 0x555fd3e35a9f in blink::HeapObjectHeader::Finalize(unsigned char*, unsigned long) third_party/blink/renderer/platform/heap/impl/heap_page.cc:95:5



<span class="line"><!---->    #5 0x555fd3e35a9f in blink::HeapObjectHeader::Finalize(unsigned char*, unsigned long) third_party/blink/renderer/platform/heap/impl/heap_page.cc:95:5<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





After document is free, CanvasRenderingContext2D object will hold a wild pointer(ukm_recorder_) which can be call from getImageInternal.



<span class="line"><!---->After document is free, CanvasRenderingContext2D object will hold a wild pointer(ukm_recorder_) which can be call from getImageInternal.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/85.0.4183.99:third_party/blink/renderer/modules/canvas/canvas2d/canvas_rendering_context_2d.cc;l=688



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/85.0.4183.99:third_party/blink/renderer/modules/canvas/canvas2d/canvas_rendering_context_2d.cc;l=688"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/85.0.4183.99:third_party/blink/renderer/modules/canvas/canvas2d/canvas_rendering_context_2d.cc;l=688<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





In master branch and version 90, the call of ukm_recorder_ is removed, but CanvasRenderingContext2D object still hold the pointer ukm_recorder_.



<span class="line"><!---->In master branch and version 90, the call of ukm_recorder_ is removed, but CanvasRenderingContext2D object still hold the pointer ukm_recorder_.<!----></span>



<br>





https://github.com/chromium/chromium/commit/809231f0c9fdc6180b6a99cf067d0a32db053034



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://github.com/chromium/chromium/commit/809231f0c9fdc6180b6a99cf067d0a32db053034"><!---->https://github.com/chromium/chromium/commit/809231f0c9fdc6180b6a99cf067d0a32db053034<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





By Search the sources, ukm_recoder_ not only hold by CanvasRenderingContext2D, but also any other objects. So problems will not only here:



<span class="line"><!---->By Search the sources, ukm_recoder_ not only hold by CanvasRenderingContext2D, but also any other objects. So problems will not only here:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/89.0.4389.88:third_party/blink/renderer/core/loader/interactive_detector.cc;l=79;



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/89.0.4389.88:third_party/blink/renderer/core/loader/interactive_detector.cc;l=79;"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/89.0.4389.88:third_party/blink/renderer/core/loader/interactive_detector.cc;l=79;<!----></a>



<br>



<br>



<br>

<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 89.0.4389.86 + stable



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 89.0.4389.86 + stable<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Ubuntu 



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Ubuntu <!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

used two conflicting sources as inputs: the CanvasRenderingContext

type, and the paint-op digest.

from the two sources, which makes it impossible to losslessly separate

the two during analysis.



<span class="line"><!---->the two during analysis.<!----></span>
